msg:The hotel address is located in the center of OCT, which is very convenient for visiting, shopping and eating. However, the service awareness reflected in parking and other issues must be a negative review. When we first arrived at the main entrance of the hotel, we told the security guard that we were staying at the hotel and asked the security guard how to park. The security guard did not arrange a parking space on the ground (we observed that there were several empty spaces). We were asked to park at Minus 3 of Yitian Holiday Plaza (same floor as the hotel). After going around, we found that the queue was ridiculously long and we couldn't move for about ten or twenty minutes. So we called the front desk of the hotel, and the front desk transferred us to some depar**ent. Only after our strong request did they agree to arrange a parking space on the ground. After getting the reply and reporting the license plate number, I squeezed out of the traffic, but the intersection behind the hotel was closed, so I had to make a twenty-minute detour before returning to the front door of the hotel. It took more than 40 minutes to arrive at the main entrance of the hotel for the first time and return for the second time. The experience was extremely poor and I was very disappointed. I was so angry that I wanted to cancel the hotel and book an InterContinental instead. Unfortunately, there was no room in the InterContinental. Everyone in the hotel is aware of the difficulty of parking during holidays. Why not arrange for idle parking spaces on the ground when you first arrive at the main entrance? Why not inform guests that they may have to queue for a long time at the mall parking lot entrance because there are no parking spaces? Is this service standard for the Westin and Marriott brands?
The room passage is much narrower than other hotels of the same level, which may be a problem in the event of a fire alarm.
The tablecloth on which the breakfast is placed is also unusual. It is actually gray and black (the color difference in the photo is much whiter). It is not easy to tell whether it is clean or unclean. Is the hotel management trying to be lazy? !
There are no trash cans in the elevator room and the lobby on the first floor. Does the hotel management want to reduce the workload and expenses?
The bathroom in the lobby needs to swipe a card to use it. Before getting the room card, the guest has to go to the lobby manager to get the card in a hurry, which is very rare! I have seen many hotels connected to shopping malls, but I have never seen anything like this.
All this shows that the management of this store lacks people-oriented and customer-oriented awareness and pursues cost first! If it weren't for the favorable location, I'm afraid it wouldn't be able to compete with other five-star hotels!

Regarding check-in, Ctrip Diamond members are required to pay a deposit when staying at this hotel. In this regard, I consulted Ctrip customer service and the hotel, and the clear answer is that there is no agreement on the waiver of the deposit deposit in the cooperation agreement between the hotel and Ctrip, and it does not apply to flash-in passengers.
Regarding the location, it is located in the upper part of Yitian Holiday Plaza in Nanshan District, opposite to the Window of the World, next to Happy Valley, Mangroves and other tourist and leisure resort areas, and the transportation to various business districts is also relatively convenient. Recommended.
Regarding hygiene, there were long hair left on the bath towels on the second day of the stay, and they were not replaced on the third day, and they did not change every day. Moreover, the burrs of the hotel towels and bath towels have been damaged, and they are hard to use, and the experience is poor.
Regarding the service, 40 minutes after complaining about the hygiene of the bath towels, no one answered. After the complaint is made clear again, the communication will be carried out. After checking and confirming that it is not my own hair, I communicated to give free breakfast and room upgrade. Delayed for 2 hours before and after, did not eat dinner.
What the guests care about most is the thoughtful and sincere service and the sincerity of showing their attitude immediately, which turned me into an unreasonable tenant who was assigned according to the order. The feeling of staying in the back is very bad.

name:M‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçe‚Äçr‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg

posted:Posted October 8, 2021
msg:The Westin Shenzhen
Surrounding environment: Located next to Yitian Holiday Mall, surrounded by Sea World, Happy Valley and Splendid China, next to the subway entrance, located in a super prime location, there are many tourists and crowds during the National Day holiday.
Hotel facilities: The decoration of the hotel is based on the positioning of the Westin Hotel, but it is mainly business-oriented.
Hotel room: The overall green tone, the room is a bit surprised without coffee machine, the design style is green to make it comfortable, and different from the feeling of urban hotels, but the overall presentation is business style.
Hotel meals: breakfast + dinner, dining location is small, in such a good location, the housing rate is very high, did not think about the design and planning, the overall style is not much, but the products are exquisite, and dinner is recommended.
Hotel services: National Day is crowded with crowds, and the speed of check-in and house cleaning is a bit chaotic. In my case, check-in is at three o'clock, and it takes about 1.5 hours to enter the room at 4:30. Many guests at the scene cannot accept that there is no room to wait for a long time. For the Marriott Hotel, it can improve the efficiency of overall room cleaning and check-in during holidays.
Overall: The location of the hotel is good, shopping mall + three tourist areas + subway entrance, parking and shopping malls are shared, and it takes more than half an hour to find a parking space. There is a slight gap between hotel planning and actual use of Westin hotels, but there is no hotel with Westin features. However, the scenery and location of the hotel are still worth recommending.
